<h3><a id="user-content-pertemuan-5---latihan" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#pertemuan-5---latihan"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Pertemuan 5 - Latihan</h3>
<p>Pada pertemuan 5 bahasa pemograman, saya diberi soal untuk latihan oleh Dosen untuk membuat Aplikasi Biodata dengan python Seperti gambar dibawah <br>

</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="print(&quot;please your full name : &quot;)
"><pre><span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"please your full name : "</span>)</pre></div>
<p>source code fiatas berfungsi untuk mencetak hasil / output berupa " <strong>please enter your full name :</strong> ". <br>
Untuk menampilkan output string, saya menggunakan <em>tanda petik dua</em> didalam fungsi print(), sedangkan jika saya ingin menampilkan output / hasil berupa angka / interger saya tidak perlu menggunakan <em>tanda petik dua</em>. Contohnya:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=" print(&quot;nama saya adalah ...&quot;)
print(1801)
"><pre> <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"nama saya adalah ..."</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1801</span>)</pre></div>
<p><br>(Seperti gambar berikut ini) <br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/noval1802/project-praktikum/blob/main/praktikum/namaot.png"><img src="/noval1802/project-praktikum/raw/main/praktikum/namaot.png" alt="Output fungsi print" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> <br></p>
<ul>
<li>Untuk source code berikutnya adalah inputan atau membuat variable. Seperti syntax dibawah ini:</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="fullname=input()
"><pre><span class="pl-s1">fullname</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">input</span>()</pre></div>
<p><strong>Keterangan :</strong> <br></p>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Variable adalah sebuah wadah penyimpanan data pada program yang akan digunakan selama program itu berjalan. Yang berfungsi sebagai variable dalam source code diatas adalah <strong>fullname</strong> . <br></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Fungsi <strong>input()</strong> adalah untuk memasukan nilai dar layar console di command prompt, lalu kemudian mengembalikan nilai saat kita menekan tombol enter <em>(newline)</em> <br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/noval1802/project-praktikum/blob/main/praktikum/hslnma.png"><img src="/noval1802/project-praktikum/raw/main/praktikum/hslnma.png" alt="input" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> <br>
Pada gambar diatas, hasil dari inputan tersebut berwarna <em>putih</em> <br></p>
</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Untuk memasukan printah lain seperti <em>Nickname, NPM, Place of bircth, Date of bircth, Year of bircth, Phone number, and address</em> mengikuti perintah yang sama seperti memasukan <em>fullname</em> <br></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Untuk menghitung rumus umur saya menggunakan variable <em>DOB</em> yaitu 2020 (Tahun sekarang) dikurangi dengan Year of bircth, pada source code berikut : <br></p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="dob=2020-year
"><pre><span class="pl-s1">dob</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">2020</span><span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-s1">year</span></pre></div>
<p>Pada syntax / source code diatas, saya menggunakan variable <em>dob</em> dimana untuk menghitung umur (variable <strong>age</strong> pada output), yaitu dengan rumus pada variable <em>dob=2020-year</em> <br></p>
<ul>
<li>Langkah kali ini saya akan menampilkan output yang diminta oleh Dosen. <br>
Output pertama yang di minta Dosen adalah menampilkan salam, yaitu dengan mengetikkan syntax / source code berikut :</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="print(&quot;\n Asalammualaikum.&quot;)
"><pre><span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"<span class="pl-cce">\n</span> Asalammualaikum."</span>)</pre></div>
<p><strong>Keterangan</strong> : <br></p>
<ol>
<li>Fungsi <strong>\n</strong> pada source code diatas adalah untuk memberi baris baru / enter / <em>newline</em></li>
<li>Fungsi print() seperti dijelaskan pada point <strong>Output</strong> diatas
Hasil source code diatas adalah seperti gambar dibawah ini : <br></li>
</ol>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/noval1802/project-praktikum/blob/main/praktikum/nma3.png"><img src="/noval1802/project-praktikum/raw/main/praktikum/nma3.png" alt="Output salam" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>Langkah terakhir menampilkan semua hasil dari inputan diatas. Dengan mengetikan source code berikut : <br></li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="print(f&quot;Let me introduce my self. My name is {fullname}, but you can call me {nickname}. My NPM {npm}. I was born in {pob} and Iam {dob} years old. I am very glad if you want to invite my house in {address}. So don't forget to call me before with the number {phone}. \n Thank You &quot;)
"><pre><span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"Let me introduce my self. My name is <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">fullname</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>, but you can call me <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">nickname</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>. My NPM <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">npm</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>. I was born in <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">pob</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> and Iam <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">dob</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> years old. <p><strong>Keterangan</strong> : <br></p>
<ul>
<li>Fungsi huruf <strong>f</strong> pada perintah <em>print(f"....")</em> adalah fungsi print atau bisa memudahkan program dalam mencetak statement dalam suatu baris dibandingkan dengan metode yang lama yaitu memisahkan string dan variable dengan symbol koma ( , ) atau plus ( + ) <br></li>
<li>Sedangkan fungsi {} pada output tersebut menampilkan hasil variable <br>
Hasil dari output tersebut seperti berikut : <br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/noval1802/project-praktikum/blob/main/praktikum/alloutput.png"><img src="/noval1802/project-praktikum/raw/main/praktikum/alloutput.png" alt="alloutput" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>
</ul>

<h3><a id="user-content-pertemuan-6---lab-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#pertemuan-6---lab-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Pertemuan 6 - lab 1</h3>
<p>Pada halaman ini (Tugas pertemuan 6 - lab 1) Saya di berikan tugas oleh Dosen yaitu mempelajari Operator Aritmatika menggunakan bahasa pemograman python. Berikut source yang di berikan oleh Dosen (<a href="/noval1802/project-praktikum/blob/main/lab1.py">source lab 1</a>)
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/noval1802/project-praktikum/blob/main/praktikum/lab1.png"><img src="/noval1802/project-praktikum/raw/main/praktikum/lab1.png" alt="Pertemmuan 6 - lab 1" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#Penggunaan End
print(&quot;A&quot;, end=&quot;&quot;)
print(&quot;B&quot;, end=&quot;&quot;)
print(&quot;C&quot;, end=&quot;&quot;)

print()
print(&quot;X&quot;)
print(&quot;Y&quot;)
print(&quot;Z&quot;)

#Penggunaan Separator
w,x,y,z=10,15,20,25
print(w,x,y,z)
print(w,x,y,z,sep=&quot;,&quot;)
print(w,x,y,z,sep=&quot;&quot;)
print(w,x,y,z,sep=&quot;:&quot;)
print(w,x,y,z,sep=&quot;-----&quot;)
"><pre><span class="pl-c">#Penggunaan End</span>
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"A"</span>, <span class="pl-s1">end</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">""</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"B"</span>, <span class="pl-s1">end</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">""</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"C"</span>, <span class="pl-s1">end</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">""</span>)

<span class="pl-en">print</span>()
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"X"</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Y"</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Z"</span>)

<span class="pl-c">#Penggunaan Separator</span>
<span class="pl-s1">w</span>,<span class="pl-s1">x</span>,<span class="pl-s1">y</span>,<span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span>,<span class="pl-c1">15</span>,<span class="pl-c1">20</span>,<span class="pl-c1">25</span>
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">w</span>,<span class="pl-s1">x</span>,<span class="pl-s1">y</span>,<span class="pl-s1">z</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">w</span>,<span class="pl-s1">x</span>,<span class="pl-s1">y</span>,<span class="pl-s1">z</span>,<span class="pl-s1">sep</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">","</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">w</span>,<span class="pl-s1">x</span>,<span class="pl-s1">y</span>,<span class="pl-s1">z</span>,<span class="pl-s1">sep</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">""</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">w</span>,<span class="pl-s1">x</span>,<span class="pl-s1">y</span>,<span class="pl-s1">z</span>,<span class="pl-s1">sep</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">":"</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">w</span>,<span class="pl-s1">x</span>,<span class="pl-s1">y</span>,<span class="pl-s1">z</span>,<span class="pl-s1">sep</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"-----"</span>)</pre></div>
<p>Oke, kali ini saya menjelaskan materi yang dijelaskan oleh Dosen. <br><br></p>
<ul>
<li>Penggunaan END
Penggunaan end digunakan untuk menambahkan kata yang dicetak di akhir baris</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="print(&quot;A&quot;, end=&quot;&quot;)
print(&quot;B&quot;, end=&quot;&quot;)
print(&quot;C&quot;, end=&quot;&quot;)
"><pre><span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"A"</span>, <span class="pl-s1">end</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">""</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"B"</span>, <span class="pl-s1">end</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">""</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"C"</span>, <span class="pl-s1">end</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">""</span>)</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>Penggunaan print() digunakan untuk mencetak output, seperti syntax dibawah ini : <br></p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="print()
"><pre><span class="pl-en">print</span>()</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>Syntax dibawah ini digunakan untuk menampilkan output berupa string</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="print(&quot;X&quot;)
print(&quot;Y&quot;)
print(&quot;Z&quot;)
"><pre><span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"X"</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Y"</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Z"</span>)</pre></div>
<p>Hasil dari source code terseut seperti gambar di bawah ini:
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/noval1802/project-praktikum/blob/main/praktikum/abcd.png"><img src="/noval1802/project-praktikum/raw/main/praktikum/abcd.png" alt="Output END" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>Pengertian separaktor
Sepaktor adalah pemisah yang berfungsi sebagai tanda pemisah antar objek yang dicetak. Defaultnya adalah tanda sepasi <br><br></li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p>Pendeklarasian beberapa variable berserta nilainya</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="w,x,y,z=10,15,20,25
"><pre><span class="pl-s1">w</span>,<span class="pl-s1">x</span>,<span class="pl-s1">y</span>,<span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span>,<span class="pl-c1">15</span>,<span class="pl-c1">20</span>,<span class="pl-c1">25</span></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>Menampilkan hasil setiap variable tiap-tiap variable</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="print(w,x,y,z)
"><pre><span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">w</span>,<span class="pl-s1">x</span>,<span class="pl-s1">y</span>,<span class="pl-s1">z</span>)</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>Menampilkan hasil variable dari tiap-tiap variable menggunakan pemisah , (koma)</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="print(w,x,y,z,sep=&quot;,&quot;)
"><pre><span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">w</span>,<span class="pl-s1">x</span>,<span class="pl-s1">y</span>,<span class="pl-s1">z</span>,<span class="pl-s1">sep</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">","</span>)</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>Menampilkan hasil variable dari tiap-tiap variable tanpa menggunakan pemisah</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="print(w,x,y,z,sep=&quot;&quot;)
"><pre><span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">w</span>,<span class="pl-s1">x</span>,<span class="pl-s1">y</span>,<span class="pl-s1">z</span>,<span class="pl-s1">sep</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">""</span>)</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>Menampilkan hasil variable dari tiap-tiap variable dengan menggunakan pemisah : (titik dua)</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="print(w,x,y,z,sep=&quot;:&quot;)
"><pre><span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">w</span>,<span class="pl-s1">x</span>,<span class="pl-s1">y</span>,<span class="pl-s1">z</span>,<span class="pl-s1">sep</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">":"</span>)</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>Menampilkan hasil variable dari tiap-tiap variable dengan menggunakan pemisah ----</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="print(w,x,y,z,sep=&quot;-----&quot;)
"><pre><span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">w</span>,<span class="pl-s1">x</span>,<span class="pl-s1">y</span>,<span class="pl-s1">z</span>,<span class="pl-s1">sep</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"-----"</span>)</pre></div>

<h3><a id="user-content-pertemuan-6---lab-1-2" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#pertemuan-6---lab-1-2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Pertemuan 6 - lab 1-2</h3>
<ul>
<li>String format <br>
String formatting atau pemformatan string memungkinkan kita menyuntikkan item kedalam string daripada kita mencoba menggabungkan string menggunakan koma atau string concatenation.<br></li>
</ul>
<p>Penggunaan pada source yang di berikan Dosen sebagai berikut : <br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/noval1802/project-praktikum/blob/main/praktikum/lab1-2.png"><img src="/noval1802/project-praktikum/raw/main/praktikum/lab1-2.png" alt="Lab 1-2" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> <br></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# string format 1
print(0, 10 ** 0)
print(1, 10 ** 1)
print(2, 10 ** 2)
print(3, 10 ** 3)
print(4, 10 ** 4)
print(5, 10 ** 5)
print(6, 10 ** 6)
print(7, 10 ** 7)
print(8, 10 ** 8)
print(9, 10 ** 9)
print(10, 10 ** 10)

# string format 2
print('{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'.format(0, 10 ** 0))
print('{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'.format(1, 10 ** 1))
print('{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'.format(2, 10 ** 2))
print('{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'.format(3, 10 ** 3))
print('{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'.format(4, 10 ** 4))
print('{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'.format(5, 10 ** 5))
print('{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'.format(6, 10 ** 6))
print('{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'.format(7, 10 ** 7))
print('{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'.format(8, 10 ** 8))
print('{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'.format(9, 10 ** 9))
print('{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'.format(10, 10 ** 10))
"><pre><span class="pl-c"># string format 1</span>

<span class="pl-c"># string format 2</span>

<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">'{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-c1">10</span> <span class="pl-c1">**</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span>))
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">'{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">10</span> <span class="pl-c1">**</span> <span class="pl-c1">4</span>))
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">'{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-c1">5</span>, <span class="pl-c1">10</span> <span class="pl-c1">**</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span>))
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">'{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-c1">6</span>, <span class="pl-c1">10</span> <span class="pl-c1">**</span> <span class="pl-c1">6</span>))
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">'{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-c1">7</span>, <span class="pl-c1">10</span> <span class="pl-c1">**</span> <span class="pl-c1">7</span>))
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">'{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-c1">8</span>, <span class="pl-c1">10</span> <span class="pl-c1">**</span> <span class="pl-c1">8</span>))

<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">'{0:&gt;3}{1:&gt;16})'</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>, <span class="pl-c1">10</span> <span class="pl-c1">**</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span>))</pre></div>
<br>
Saat ini saya akan menjelaskan satu persatu dari syntax yang diberikan oleh Dosen <br>
<ol>
<li><strong>String format 1</strong> <br>
Pada syntax / source code string format 1 akan menampilkan output berupa 2 outputan. <br>
Yang pertama (sebelah kiri) akan menampilkan angka urut dari angka 0 hingga 10, sedangkan sebelah kanan akan menampilkan Oprasi Aritmatika Pangkat. <br>
Dengan ketentuan sebagau berikut, oprasi pangkat dengan angka kiri sebagai pokok (Rumus : ** [Bintang dua]) <br>
Hasil dari syntax tersebut adalah 10 pangkat 0, hingga 10 pangkat 10. Dengan output sebagai berikut : <br></li>
</ol>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/noval1802/project-praktikum/blob/main/praktikum/pangkat.png"><img src="/noval1802/project-praktikum/raw/main/praktikum/pangkat.png" alt="Operasi Aritmatika pangkat **" style="max-width: 100%;"></a><br><br></p>
<ol start="2">
<li><strong>String Format 2</strong> <br><br>
Pada syntax / source code string format 2 akan menampilkan output berupa 2 output'an juga (Seoerti string format 1, yaitu kanan dan kiri) <br>
Dengan ketentuan sebagai berikut : <br></li>
</ol>
<blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>Alignment, padding, dan precesion dengan <strong>.format()</strong> dalam kurung kurawal kita dapat menetapkan panjang bidang, rata kanan/kiri, parameter pembulatan dan banyak lagi. Contoh lain seperti berikut :</p>
</blockquote>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="print('{0:8} | {1:9}'.format('sepatu','Jumlah'))
print('{0:8} | {1:9}'.format('dalas', 3.))
print('{0:8} | {1:9}'.format('NB',10))
"><pre><span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">'{0:8} | {1:9}'</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-s">'sepatu'</span>,<span class="pl-s">'Jumlah'</span>))
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">'{0:8} | {1:9}'</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-s">'dalas'</span>, <span class="pl-c1">3.</span>))
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">'{0:8} | {1:9}'</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-s">'NB'</span>,<span class="pl-c1">10</span>))</pre></div>
<p>Hasil dari source code contoh di atas akan seperti berikut : <br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/noval1802/project-praktikum/blob/main/praktikum/nb.png"><img src="/noval1802/project-praktikum/raw/main/praktikum/nb.png" alt="OutPut Aligmnent contoh" style="max-width: 100%;"></a><br><br></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Secara default, <strong>.format()</strong> menggunakan rata text kiri, angka ke kanan. &lt;,^, atau &gt; untuk perataan kiri, tengah , atau kanan. Contoh lain dari penggunaan <strong>.format()</strong> sebagai berikut : <br></p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="print('{:&lt;30}{:^30}{:&gt;30}'.format('Kiri','Tengah','Kanan'))
print('{:&lt;30}{:^30}{:&gt;30}'.format(12,34,56))
"><pre><span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">'{:&lt;30}{:^30}{:&gt;30}'</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-s">'Kiri'</span>,<span class="pl-s">'Tengah'</span>,<span class="pl-s">'Kanan'</span>))
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">'{:&lt;30}{:^30}{:&gt;30}'</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-c1">12</span>,<span class="pl-c1">34</span>,<span class="pl-c1">56</span>))</pre></div>
<p>Hasil dari source code contohdiatas akan muncul seperti ini : <br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/noval1802/project-praktikum/blob/main/praktikum/rata.png"><img src="/noval1802/project-praktikum/raw/main/praktikum/rata.png" alt="Output Alignment" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<br>

Hasil string format 2 adalah : <br>

<h3><a id="user-content-pertemuan-6---lab-2" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#pertemuan-6---lab-2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Pertemuan 6 - Lab 2</h3>
<ul>
<li>Konversi Nilai Variable
Untuk pembahasan terakhir, kali ini akan myenyelesaikan tugas Lab 2 dari Dosen, yaitu Konversi Nilai Variable <br>
Tugas yang di berikan oleh Dosen adalah seperti gambar dibawah ini atau bisa di temukan dengan link berikut : (<a href="/noval1802/project-praktikum/blob/main/lab%202.py">temukan</a>)
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/noval1802/project-praktikum/blob/main/praktikum/Lab2.png"><img src="/noval1802/project-praktikum/raw/main/praktikum/Lab2.png" alt="pertemuan 6 lab 2" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="a=int(input(&quot;Masukkan Nilai A : &quot;))
b=int(input(&quot;Masukkan Nilai B : &quot;))
print(&quot;Variable A : &quot;,a)
print(&quot;Variable B : &quot;,b)
print(&quot;Hasil penggabungan {1}&amp;{0}=%d&quot;.format(a,b) %(a+b))

#Konversi nilai variable
a=int(a)
b=int(b)
print(&quot;Hasil penjumlahan {1}+{0}=%d&quot;.format(a,b) %(a+b))
print(&quot;Hasil pembagian {1}/{0}=%d&quot;.format(a,b) %(a/b))
"><pre><span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">int</span>(<span class="pl-en">input</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Masukkan Nilai A : "</span>))
<span class="pl-s1">b</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">int</span>(<span class="pl-en">input</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Masukkan Nilai B : "</span>))
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Variable A : "</span>,<span class="pl-s1">a</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Variable B : "</span>,<span class="pl-s1">b</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Hasil penggabungan {1}&amp;{0}=%d"</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-s1">a</span>,<span class="pl-s1">b</span>) <span class="pl-c1">%</span>(<span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-c1">+</span><span class="pl-s1">b</span>))

<span class="pl-c">#Konversi nilai variable</span>
<span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">int</span>(<span class="pl-s1">a</span>)
<span class="pl-s1">b</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">int</span>(<span class="pl-s1">b</span>)
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Hasil penjumlahan {1}+{0}=%d"</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-s1">a</span>,<span class="pl-s1">b</span>) <span class="pl-c1">%</span>(<span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-c1">+</span><span class="pl-s1">b</span>))
<span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Hasil pembagian {1}/{0}=%d"</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-s1">a</span>,<span class="pl-s1">b</span>) <span class="pl-c1">%</span>(<span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-s1">b</span>))</pre></div>
<br>
Hasil dari source / code diatas : <br>
